=== FULL EXTRACTED CONTENT ===


--- [John Mylopoulos - Wikipedia] ---
John Mylopoulos (born 12 July 1943) is a Greek-Canadian computer scientist, Professor at the University of Toronto, Canada, and at the University of Trento, Italy. He is known for his work in the field of conceptual modeling, specifically the development of an agent-oriented software development methodology. called TROPOS.


--- [John Mylopoulos' Web Page] ---
&lt;table border="1" cellpadding="20"&gt; &lt;td&gt;&lt;a href="http://www.toronto.edu"&gt;&lt;img src="utcrest89.gif" width="75" length="150"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt; &lt;td&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;center&gt;&lt;font valign = "top" color="darkblue" size="8" face="Bertram LET"&gt;JOHN MYLOPOULOS&lt;/font&gt;&lt;center&gt;&lt;/td&gt; &lt;/table&gt; &lt;/head&gt; &lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt; &lt;table cellpadding="5"&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td&gt; &lt;img src="JMylo.jpg" width="200" length="400" border="5"&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;td&gt; &lt;b&gt;&lt;font size="4" face="Espy Sans Bold"&gt; &lt;br&gt;Department of Computer Science &lt;br&gt;University of Toronto &lt;br&gt;40 St.George St. &lt;br&gt;Bahen Building Rm.7266 &lt;br&gt;University of Toronto &lt;br&gt;Toronto, Ontario &lt;br&gt;M5S 2E4 &lt;p&gt;Tel: 416-978-5180 &lt;br&gt;Fax: 416-978-4765 &lt;br&gt;Email: &lt;b&gt;&lt;font color="#000066"&gt;jm@cs.toronto.edu&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/font&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;/table&gt; &lt;table&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;font size="2" face="Helvetica"&gt; &lt;h2&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;a name = "Biography"&gt;Biography&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/h2&gt; &lt;P&gt; John Mylopoulos received his BEng degree from Brown University in 1966 and his PhD degree from Princeton in 1970, the year he joined the faculty of the University of Toronto. His research interests include information modelling techniques, covering notations, implementation techniques and applications, knowledge based systems, semantic data models, information system design and requirements engineering. &lt;/P&gt; &lt;P&gt; Mylopoulos is the recipient of the first Outstanding Services Award given by the Canadian AI Society (CSCSI), a co-recipient of the best-paper award of the 1994 International Conference on Software Engineering, a fellow of the American Association for AI (AAAI) and the elected president of the &lt;a href = "http://www.vldb.org"&gt;VLDB&lt;/a&gt; Endowment (1998-01, re-elected for the period 2002-05). He is co-editor of the Requirements Engineering Journal, published by Springer-Verlag. He has also contributed to the organization of major international conferences, including program co-chair of the International Joint Conference of AI (1991), general chair of the Entity-Relationship conference (1994), program chair of the International IEEE Symposium of Requirements Engineering (1997), and general chair of the 30th VLDB Conference (2004). He has served on the editorial board of several international journals.&lt;/P&gt; &lt;P&gt; He is currently leading a number of research projects and is principal investigator of both a national and a provincial Centre of Excellence. In particular, he leads a project on software reengineering (funded by NSERC, IBM Canada and Bell University Laboratories), a project on Knowledge Management (funded by Bell University Laboratories, PRECARN and Techne Knowledge Systems) , as well as a project on Peer-to-Peer Data Management (funded by CITO, NSERC, and Bell University Laboratories.) &lt;/P&gt; &lt;/font&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td&gt; &lt;font size="2" face="Helvetica"&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;h2&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;&lt;a name = "Selected Publications"&gt;Selected Publications:&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/h2&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&amp;nbspRoussopoulos, N., Mylopoulos, J., "Using Semantic Networks for Database Management", Proceedings of the First International Conference on Very Large Databases, September 1975, 144-172. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;li&gt;&amp;nbspMylopoulos, J., Bernstein, P. and Wong, H., "A language facility for designing interactive database-intensive applications", ACM Transactions on Database Systems 5(2), June 1980. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;li&gt;&amp;nbspGreenspan, S., Mylopoulos, J. and Borgida, A., "Capturing more world knowledge in the requirements specification", in the Proceedings of the Sixth International Conference on Software Engineering, Tokyo, 1982. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;li&gt;&amp;nbspBrodie, M., Mylopoulos, J. and Schmidt, J.,(eds.) On Conceptual Modelling: Perspectives from Artificial Intelligence, Databases and Programming Languages, Springer Verlag, 1984. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;li&gt;&amp;nbspMylopoulos, J., Borgida, A., Jarke, M. and Koubarakis, M., "Telos: Representing Knowledge About Information Systems" ACM Transactions on Information Systems 8(4), October 1990. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;li&gt;&amp;nbspBorgida, A., Mylopoulos, J. and Reiter R., "On the frame problem in procedure specifications", IEEE Transactions on Software Engineering, October 1995. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;li&gt;&amp;nbspGal, A., Kerr, S., and Mylopoulos, J., "Information Services for the Web: Building and Maintaining Domain Models", International Journal of Cooperative Information Systems 8(4), December 1999, 227-254 &lt;/li&gt; --- [John Mylopoulos | Faculté de génie - University of Ottawa] ---
Le professeur Mylopoulos est actuellement chercheur invité à l'Université d'Ottawa. Il a obtenu son BEng à l'université de Brown en 1966 et son PhD à Princeton en 1970, année où il a rejoint la faculté de l'université de Toronto. Ses recherches portent sur l'ingénierie des exigences, la sémantique des données et la gestion des connaissances. Il a pris sa retraite de Toronto en 2009 et a rejoint l'Université de Trento (Italie) où il a dirigé un grand projet européen sur le génie logiciel (2011-16). M. Mylopoulos a reçu le premier prix Outstanding Services Award décerné par la Société canadienne d'intelligence artificielle (1992), il est co-récipiendaire du prix du papier le plus influent de la Conférence internationale sur le génie logiciel de 1994, il est membre de l'Association américaine d'intelligence artificielle (AAAI), il a été élu président du VLDB Endowment (1998-01, réélu pour la période 2002-05) et il est membre de la Société royale du Canada.
